< review>
This river is along highway scenic 299 in northern California. This a drive you want to go slow to be able to observe the beauty.  There are slow vehicles turn outs every few miles. Let those in a hurry go around you and enjoy. Take advantage of the many vista points you can stop at. Life is to short to hurry and miss this gift i9</review>

5< /rate>
< text>
HWY 299 is a twisting and turning highway. But, the scenic route and the people along the way make the effort worth every mile. Plenty of pullouts. Gas stations are located at Willow Creek and Weaverville.   Cell phone service is patchy, but can be found at Willow Creek, Weaverville, and Junction City. I'm NOT sure about Douglas though.</text>

<Text>I have been going to BigBrand for several years now. They attracted me as a customer with free flat repairs, free tire rotations, and low price guarantee.

The problem with free rotations and flat repairs is the wait, always 1 hour minimum for a 5 minute job. Obviously they want to sell you new tires every time you come in for a free service. I bought 4 kumos (70k mile warranty) for my Acura at their shop and after 30k miles I went in for another rotation and they wouldn't rotate and said I need new tires. I wasn't offered any warranty assistance.

Last month I needed tires for my Mazda and asked them to price match tire buyer dot com on a set of Firestone Firehawk Indy 500. They couldn't beat the price and would only get within  about $40 of it. I wasn't offered a free set of tires like they advertise as you can see in my attached photo.

Today I went in for an oil change I had an appointment at 9AM. My first red flag went up when he asked if I was going to wait for it, of course it's an oil change takes me 20 minutes to do myself.  I asked if it was going to be a while and was told it would be done within the hour. Well at 936AM my car finally moves into the shop. Next red flag goes up when I watch the lube tech look under the hood for a few minutes with confusion.  I go out there and ask him if he is looking for tor filter location and he said yes. I told him it is under the car near the drain plug.  At 1015AM I am told by the salesperson that they cannot get the old oil filter off.  I asked if they can have a more experienced person try, so he said he would get "The Mechanic" to try. They have 10 people working on cars out there but only one is a mechanic? The mechanic gets the filter off in under 30 seconds and returns to his work.  They spend 30 more minutes refilling the oil, replacing filter,  and resetting the oil monitor. At 1045AM the job is done. Almost 2 hours for an oil change AND I had an appointment!

I would recommend you only take your vehicle here if you can drop it off for a day or two and not care how long it takes them.  There are a few other places in town that offer the same free rotations, flat repairs, and low price guarantees. I might be going to a different store from now on.</Text>< Pictures>

< Review>
I don't usually write reviews, but my experience at the Santa Maria Big Brand Tire was negative enough that I feel it's worth sharing. I went in today for a set of new tires. After signing the paperwork I was told that they were a little behind schedule so it would be about 1.5 hours before I would get my car back. When scheduling the appointment I had seen a web page describing a "50/50 challenge" (tire change in 50 minutes or you get $50 off). So, naturally, I mentioned that I'd seen that online and I was wondering if that applied. The attendant at the desk asked me to wait for a moment while he went into the shop and, when he returned, told me they would do what they could to finish the job in under 50 minutes.

Fast forward 32 minutes later... I hear my name and walk up to the counter. They finished 18 minutes early! I was impressed, to say the least.  However, that's when my mood changed. When I got to the counter a worker from the shop (who I assumed was the manager, but didn't confirm) poked his head in to ask if they beat the 50/50 challenge. When it's confirmed that they did he made a point of loudly saying (i'm paraphrasing) "Of course, because we pushed back everyone else" so that everyone in the waiting room could hear, making me look like a jerk. I was then informed by the attendant that the 50/50 usually needs to be requested when the online appointment is made, that way they can plan accordingly.

As a customer, it isn't my job to know the ins and outs of Big Brand Tire's policies. I'm an easy going guy. If they had told me when I arrived that I needed to mention the 50/50 challenge when I booked the appointment, oh well, I would've been sure to do it the next time. Unfortunately for them, there wont be a next time. The way the manager(?) rudely announced to everyone that I was making them late was unprofessional and immature. I had just spent over $500 at their business and I was immediately put down because THEY had not informed me about THEIR business policies when I had first arrived.

Normally I would give them 1 star, but I'm giving them 2 because they did finish the job early and the attendant I spent most of the time speaking to was calm, collected, and courteous (unlike the other guy!). I'll let them have the second star for that because they won't be getting my business again.

**Note to anyone that still decides to go here: Make sure you call them when making an appointment and mention the 50/50 challenge! That way you won't get stuck with a long wait time like some of the other commenters (or at least you'll get $50 off your purchase!)**< /Review>
